рддрддреНрд░рд╛рджреМ рд╡рд┐рд╡рд┐рдзрдорддрд╛рдХреБрд▓рд┐рддрджреАрдХреНрд╖рд╛рд╡рд┐рдзрд┐рд▓рд┐рдЦрдиреЗ рдкрд░рдорд╛рд╢рдХреНрддрд╕реНрдпрд╛рдкреНрдпреН4 рдЖрддреНрдордиреЛ рднрдЧрд╡рджрдиреБрдЧреНрд░рд╣реЗрдг рд╢рдХреНрддрддрд╛рдВ рд╕рдореН5рднрд╛рд╡рдпрдиреНрдиреН рдЗрд╡ рдкреНрд░рд╛рд░рд┐рдкреНрд╕рд┐рддрд╕рд┐рджреНрдзрдпреЗ рдкреВрд░реНрд╡рд╡рджреН рдЧреБрд░реБрд░реВрдкрдореН рдЗрд╖реНрдЯрджреИрд╡рддрдВ рдкреНрд░рдгрдорддрд┐ рддрдореН рдЗрддрд┐ ред рд╢реНрд░реАрдорд╛рдиреН рдХреГрд╖реНрдгрд╢реН6 рдЪрд╛рд╕реМ рдЪреИрддрдиреНрдпрджреЗрд╡рд╢реН рдЪ7 рдкрд░рдорд╛рддреНрдореЗрддрд┐ рддрдореН ред рдкрдХреНрд╖реЗ рд╢реНрд░реАрдХреГрд╖реНрдгрдЪреИрддрдиреНрдпреЗрддрд┐ рдЦреНрдпрд╛рддрдВ рджреЗрд╡рдореН8 рдИрд╢реНрд╡рд░рдореН ред рд╕рд╛рдХреНрд╖рд╛рддреН рддрд╕реНрдпреЛрдкрджреЗрд╖реНрдЯреГрддреНрд╡рд╛рд╕рдореНрднрд╡реЗ рд╜рдкрд┐ рдЪрд┐рддреНрддрд╛рдзрд┐рд╖реНрдард╛рддреГрддреНрд╡рд╛рджрд┐рдирд╛ рд╕рд░реНрд╡реЗрд╖рд╛рдореН рдЕрдкрд┐ рдЬреАрд╡рд╛рдирд╛рдВ рдкрд░рдордЧреБрд░реБрддрдпрд╛рдордиреЛ рд╜рдкрд┐ рд╕ рдПрд╡ рдЧреБрд░реБрд░реН рдЗрддреНрдпреН рдЕрднрд┐рдкреНрд░реЗрддреНрдп рд▓рд┐рдЦрддрд┐ рдЬрдЧрджреНрдЧреБрд░реБрдореН рдЗрддрд┐9 ред рдкрдХреНрд╖реЗ рд╕рд░реНрд╡рддреНрд░реИрд╡10 рднрдЧрд╡рдиреНрдирд╛рдорд╕рдВрдХреАрд░реНрддрдирдкреНрд░рдзрд╛рдирднрдХреНрддрд┐рдкреНрд░рдЪрд╛рд░рдгрд╛рдЬреН рдЬрдЧрддрд╛рдВ рдЧреБрд░реБрддреНрд╡реЗрди рд╡рд┐рд╢реЗрд╖рддреЛ рджреАрдирдЬрдирд╡рд┐рд╖рдпрдХрд╕рдордЧреНрд░реЛрдкрджреЗрд╢рд╛рдиреБрдЧреНрд░рд╣рдгреЗ рдЧреБрд░реБрдореН рдЗрддрд┐ реерез рее

рдЕрде рджреАрдХреНрд╖рд╛рд╡рд┐рдзрд┐рдГ

рджреАрдХреНрд╖рд╛рд╡рд┐рдзрд┐рд░реН рд▓рд┐рдЦреНрдпрддреЗ рд╜рддреНрд░рд╛рдиреБрд╕реГрддреНрдп рдХреНрд░рдорджреАрдкрд┐рдХрд╛рдореН11 ред

рд╡рд┐рдирд╛ рджреАрдХреНрд╖рд╛рдВ рд╣рд┐ рдкреВрдЬрд╛рдпрд╛рдВ рдирд╛рдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░реЛ рд╜рд╕реНрддрд┐ рдХрд╕реНрдпрдЪрд┐рддреН реереи рее

Broo

Chapter Two: On Initiation

┬╣I worship this blessed Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зacaitanyadeva, the preceptor of the world, by whose grace even a dog can easily cross a great ocean.

DDс╣м:[^FNB000113]

I worship the master ┼Ъr─л Caitanya, by whose power a blind man sees the scriptures and a stone crosses the ocean. Knowledge of part of oneтАЩs duties will inevitably be [erroneously] accepted in total; therefore, whatever is abbreviated elsewhere, this book expounds in detail.

Now, at the beginning, in describing the rules for initiation, bewildered by many different opinions, the author in this verse as before pays homage to his beloved Lord in the form of the preceptor. By this he empowers himself, as it were, by the grace of the Lord, even though himself most incompetent, to accomplish that which he has intended to begin. [I worship] this blessed Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa, Caitanyadeva, the supreme self. Or else, the deva or master known as Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зacaitanya. The author writes preceptor of the world to indicate that even if one does not have him directly as a teacher, he only is the preceptor of every living being, since he superintends the intellect. Or in his own view, he is the preceptor, as he has the office of the teacher, particularly through the favour of his complete teachings relating to the fallen people of the world, by teaching devotion primarily characterised by congregational chanting of the LordтАЩs names everywhere.

Rules for Initiation

┬▓The rules for initiation are written here, following the Kramad─лpik─Б, for without initiation, nobody has the eligibility for performing worship.

рддрдВ рд╢реНрд░реАрдорддреНрдХреГрд╖реНрдгрдЪреИрддрдиреНрдпрджреЗрд╡рдВ рд╡рдиреНрджреЗ рдЬрдЧрджреНрдЧреБрд░реБрдореН ред

рдпрд╕реНрдпрд╛рдиреБрдХрдореНрдкрдпрд╛ рд╢реНрд╡рд╛рдкрд┐ рдорд╣рд╛рдмреНрдзрд┐рдВ рд╕рдиреНрддрд░реЗрддреН рд╕реБрдЦрдореН1 реерез рее

рдЕрдиреНрдзрдГ2 рдкрд╢реНрдпрддрд┐ рд╢рд╛рд╕реНрддреНрд░рд╛рдгрд┐ рд╢рд┐рд▓рд╛ рддрд░рддрд┐ рд╡рд╛рд░рд┐рдзрд┐рдореН ред

рдпрд╕реНрдп рдкреНрд░рднрд╛рд╡рддреЛ рд╡рдиреНрджреЗ рддрдВ рд╢реНрд░реАрдЪреИрддрдиреНрдпрдореН рдИрд╢реНрд╡рд░рдореН рее

рдХрд░реНрддрд╡реНрдпрд╛рдВрд╢рд╕реНрдп3 рд╡рд┐рдЬреНрдЮрд╛рдирдореН рдЕрд╡рд╢реНрдпрдВ рд╕рдореНрдпрдЧреН рдЗрд╖реНрдпрддреЗ ред

рдЕрддреЛ рдпрд╕реН рддрддреНрд░ рд╕рдВрдХреНрд╖рд┐рдкреНрддреЛ рдЧреНрд░рдиреНрдердГ рд╕реЛ рд╜рдпрдВ рдкреНрд░рдкрдЮреНрдЪреНрдпрддреЗ рее

рддрддреНрд░рд╛рджреМ рд╡рд┐рд╡рд┐рдзрдорддрд╛рдХреБрд▓рд┐рддрджреАрдХреНрд╖рд╛рд╡рд┐рдзрд┐рд▓рд┐рдЦрдиреЗ рдкрд░рдорд╛рд╢рдХреНрддрд╕реНрдпрд╛рдкреНрдпреН4 рдЖрддреНрдордиреЛ рднрдЧрд╡рджрдиреБрдЧреНрд░рд╣реЗрдг рд╢рдХреНрддрддрд╛рдВ рд╕рдореН5рднрд╛рд╡рдпрдиреНрдиреН рдЗрд╡ рдкреНрд░рд╛рд░рд┐рдкреНрд╕рд┐рддрд╕рд┐рджреНрдзрдпреЗ рдкреВрд░реНрд╡рд╡рджреН рдЧреБрд░реБрд░реВрдкрдореН рдЗрд╖реНрдЯрджреИрд╡рддрдВ рдкреНрд░рдгрдорддрд┐ рддрдореН рдЗрддрд┐ ред рд╢реНрд░реАрдорд╛рдиреН рдХреГрд╖реНрдгрд╢реН6 рдЪрд╛рд╕реМ рдЪреИрддрдиреНрдпрджреЗрд╡рд╢реН рдЪ7 рдкрд░рдорд╛рддреНрдореЗрддрд┐ рддрдореН ред рдкрдХреНрд╖реЗ рд╢реНрд░реАрдХреГрд╖реНрдгрдЪреИрддрдиреНрдпреЗрддрд┐ рдЦреНрдпрд╛рддрдВ рджреЗрд╡рдореН8 рдИрд╢реНрд╡рд░рдореН ред рд╕рд╛рдХреНрд╖рд╛рддреН рддрд╕реНрдпреЛрдкрджреЗрд╖реНрдЯреГрддреНрд╡рд╛рд╕рдореНрднрд╡реЗ рд╜рдкрд┐ рдЪрд┐рддреНрддрд╛рдзрд┐рд╖реНрдард╛рддреГрддреНрд╡рд╛рджрд┐рдирд╛ рд╕рд░реНрд╡реЗрд╖рд╛рдореН рдЕрдкрд┐ рдЬреАрд╡рд╛рдирд╛рдВ рдкрд░рдордЧреБрд░реБрддрдпрд╛рдордиреЛ рд╜рдкрд┐ рд╕ рдПрд╡ рдЧреБрд░реБрд░реН рдЗрддреНрдпреН рдЕрднрд┐рдкреНрд░реЗрддреНрдп рд▓рд┐рдЦрддрд┐ рдЬрдЧрджреНрдЧреБрд░реБрдореН рдЗрддрд┐9 ред рдкрдХреНрд╖реЗ рд╕рд░реНрд╡рддреНрд░реИрд╡10 рднрдЧрд╡рдиреНрдирд╛рдорд╕рдВрдХреАрд░реНрддрдирдкреНрд░рдзрд╛рдирднрдХреНрддрд┐рдкреНрд░рдЪрд╛рд░рдгрд╛рдЬреН рдЬрдЧрддрд╛рдВ рдЧреБрд░реБрддреНрд╡реЗрди рд╡рд┐рд╢реЗрд╖рддреЛ рджреАрдирдЬрдирд╡рд┐рд╖рдпрдХрд╕рдордЧреНрд░реЛрдкрджреЗрд╢рд╛рдиреБрдЧреНрд░рд╣рдгреЗ рдЧреБрд░реБрдореН рдЗрддрд┐ реерез рее

рдЕрде рджреАрдХреНрд╖рд╛рд╡рд┐рдзрд┐рдГ

рджреАрдХреНрд╖рд╛рд╡рд┐рдзрд┐рд░реН рд▓рд┐рдЦреНрдпрддреЗ рд╜рддреНрд░рд╛рдиреБрд╕реГрддреНрдп рдХреНрд░рдорджреАрдкрд┐рдХрд╛рдореН11 ред

рд╡рд┐рдирд╛ рджреАрдХреНрд╖рд╛рдВ рд╣рд┐ рдкреВрдЬрд╛рдпрд╛рдВ рдирд╛рдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░реЛ рд╜рд╕реНрддрд┐ рдХрд╕реНрдпрдЪрд┐рддреН реереи рее

рдХреНрд░рдорджреАрдкрд┐рдХрд╛рдореН рдЕрдиреБрд╕реГрддреНрдпреЗрддрд┐ рд╢реНрд░реАрдХреЗрд╢рд╡рд╛рдЪрд╛рд░реНрдпрд╡рд┐рд░рдЪрд┐рддрдХреНрд░рдорджреАрдкрд┐рдХрд╛рдЦреНрдпрдЧреНрд░рдиреНрдереЛрдХреНрддрд╛рдиреБрд╕рд╛рд░реЗрдгреИрд╡, рди рддреБ рддрджреБрдХреНрддрд╡рд┐рд░реЛрдзреЗрдиреЗрддреНрдпреН12 рдЕрд░реНрдердГ ред рджреАрдХреНрд╖рд╛рд╡рд┐рдзрд┐рд▓рд┐рдЦрдиреЗ рд╣реЗрддреБрдГ13 рд╡рд┐рдиреЗрддрд┐ ред рд╣рд┐ рдпрддрдГ14 реереирее

рдЕрде рджреАрдХреНрд╖рд╛рдирд┐рддреНрдпрддрд╛

рдЖрдЧрдореЗтАФ15

рджреНрд╡рд┐рдЬрд╛рдирд╛рдореН рдЕрдиреБрдкреЗрддрд╛рдирд╛рдВ рд╕реНрд╡рдХрд░реНрдорд╛рдзреНрдпрдпрдирд╛рджрд┐рд╖реБ ред

Broo

Following the Kramad─лpik─Б: according to the statements of the book called Kramad─лpik─Б, written by Ke┼Ыava ─Аc─Бrya, and not in contradiction to its statements. That is the meaning. The reason for giving the rules for initiation is indicated by [the clause beginning with] for without. For is used in the sense of тАЬsinceтАЭ.

The Mandatoriness of Initiation

In the ─Аgama:[^FNB000114]

┬│Just as Br─Бhmaс╣Зas who have not been ordained do not have the eligibility for their own duties of Vedic study and so on, but possess it after Upanayana, тБ┤so those who are not initiated do not have the eligibility for mantras, worship of gods and so on. Therefore, make yourself praised by ┼Ъiva!

Have not studied means those who have not undergone the Upanayana ceremony, as after Upanayana or receiving the sacrificial thread one becomes eligible. Praised by ┼Ъiva means initiated. The implied meaning is that by the pre-eminence of accepting Viс╣гс╣Зu initiation, one becomes the object of the great praise even of ┼Ъiva. And further, without initiation, one is not eligible for performing worship. As it is said,[^FNB000115] тАЬOne who eats anything before worshipping the ┼Ъ─Бlagr─Бma stone becomes a worm in the stool of dog-eaters for an eon.тАЭ From statements such as this, the necessity of worship and the mandatoriness of initiation is established. Because the ┼Ъ─Бlagr─Бma stone is foremost among the objects of the Lord, all of the objects of the Lord are implied.[^FNB000116]

In a conversation between Brahm─Б and N─Бrada in connection with the month of K─Бrttika in the Skanda Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):

тБ╡Those men who have not received Vaiс╣гс╣Зava initiation or who do not worship Jan─Бrdana are animals in this world. What is the use of their lives?

Broo

The author establishes its mandatoriness with this statement of Brahm─БтАЩs. Who do not worship Jan─Бrdana: since ritualistic worship will be a failure without initiation.

In the same book, in a conversation between Rukm─Бс╣Еgada and Mohin─л (тАУ), and in the Viс╣гс╣Зu Y─Бmala:

тБ╢O woman of handsome thighs, all that the uninitiated does is useless: without initiation, a person will be reborn as an animal.

The specifics are given in the Viс╣гс╣Зu Y─Бmala:

тБ╖If it is taken without initiation, out of affection or out of greed, a divine curse will fall on both the preceptor and the disciple.

Without initiation: without following the rules for initiation. A divine curse: the curse of all the divinities or the curse of the presiding deity of the mantra.

Even though it follows from what has earlier been stated about the mandatoriness of approaching a preceptor (1.36тАУ37) that also initiation is mandatory, still, since one might think that approaching [the preceptor] might entail only taking shelter of him, initiation, that is, accepting a mantra in the correct way, and so on, is separately mentioned. This is the drift.

And in the Viс╣гс╣Зurahasya:[^FNB000117]

тБ╕One who engages in devotion without having understood the statements about the performance of the rules of worship of Hari will according to the precepts attain a hundredth part.

Now, one may hear about the great result of engaging in ritualistic worship of the Lord in any way. Therefore, why insist on this accepting of initiation from a guru? To this the author replies with this verse. One who according to the precepts engages in devotion without having understood, having not at all apprehended from the preceptor the statements, the proper teachings of generations of earlier teachers about the performance or undertaking of the rules of worship of Hari, will attain only one of a hundred parts. The Greatness of Initiation

In the Viс╣гс╣Зu Y─Бmala:[^FNB000118]

тБ╣Since it awards divine [divyam] knowledge and effects the destruction [saс╣Гkс╣гaya] of sin, it is called initiation [d─лkс╣г─Б] by the guides conversant with the truth. ┬╣тБ░Therefore, bowing to the guru and offering him everything, one should accept a Vaiс╣гс╣Зava mantra from him along with initiation according to the precepts.

Strenghtening its mandatoriness and showing how it affords a particular result even though it is mandatory, just like the Dar┼Ыapaurс╣Зam─Бsa and other sacrifices, the author describes the greatness of initiation in this and the two following quotations.[^FNB000119]

In a discussion between Brahm─Б and N─Бrada in the same place of the Skanda Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):

┬╣┬╣Those foremost men on earth, who have accepted Vaiс╣гс╣Зava initiation, remover of all suffering, are both ascetics and devoted to their duties.

Foremost means superior to those devoted to knowledge and so on.

And in the Tattvas─Бgara:

┬╣┬▓Just as bell-metal turns into gold by the application of mercury, so men become twice-born by the method of initiation.

All men become twice-born, Br─Бhmaс╣Зas [by initiation].

Consideration of Months

In the ─Аgama:[^FNB000120]

┬╣┬│Accepting a mantra in [the month of] Caitra gives much suffering; in Vai┼Ы─Бkha, one attains riches; in Jyaiс╣гс╣нha, certain death; ┬╣тБ┤in ─Ас╣г─Бdha, the destruction of friends; in ┼Ъr─Бvaс╣Зa, terror; in Bh─Бdrapada, the death of oneтАЩs offspring; auspiciousness everywhere in ─А┼Ыvina; ┬╣тБ╡in K─Бrttika, increase of wealth, in M─Бrga┼Ы─лrс╣гa, auspiciousness; in Pauс╣гa, the destruction of knowledge; in M─Бgha, the increase of wisdom; in Ph─Бlguna, mastery over allтАФthis the preceptors have proclaimed.

And somewhere:[^FNB000121]

┬╣тБ╢In ┼Ъr─Бvaс╣Зa there will assuredly be prosperity; in K─Бrttika, knowledge; in Ph─Бlguna there will be prosperity as well. The impure month[^FNB000122] should be avoided.

And somewhere, in the R─Бm─Бrcanacandrik─Б, following the Agastya Saс╣Гhit─Б (17.7тАУ9ab). The contradictions from what has already been stated should be understood to stem from the differences between various mantras, the considerations of various rules and results, or from differences of opinion. Similarly below as well.

In a discussion between Rukm─Бс╣Еgada and Mohin─л in the same place of the Skanda Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):

┬╣тБ╖But initiation done in K─Бrttika cuts the rebirth of men! Therefore, with all effort, initiation should be done in K─Бrttika.

┬╣тБ╕But there can be no contamination in initiation into the blessed Gop─Бla mantras. Because the guides have said тАЬin the month of CaitraтАЭ, therefore, initiation [should be performed] then only.

Now, even though Caitra was forbidden (in 2.13), the author permits initiation into the blessed Gop─Бla mantra with this verse. [тАж] Ke┼Ыava ─Аc─Бrya and others have said so. Therefore, in the Kramad─лpik─Б (5.1), тАЬThis ritual should be done in the month of CaitraтАЭ. And in the Trailokyasammohana Tantra: тАЬWhen the month of Caitra appears, one should fast on the Dv─Бda┼Ы─л of the waxing fortnight and thus become completely pure.тАЭ

┬▓тБ░Rohiс╣З─л, ┼Ъravaс╣З─Б, ─Аrdr─Б, Dhaniс╣гс╣нh─Б, the three Uttaras,[^FNB000125] Puс╣гya, and ┼Ъatabhiс╣гaтАФthese are the lunar mansions for initiation.

And somewhere:[^FNB000126]

┬▓┬╣One should anoint with a mantra during A┼Ыvin─л, Rohiс╣З─л, Sv─Бti, Vi┼Ы─Бkh─Б, Hasta, Jyeс╣гс╣нh─Б or the three Uttaras.

Even though this list A┼Ыvin─л and so on contradicts the previous one, this verse gives the procedure for attaining a particular result. Similarly below as well. Anoint with a mantra means initiate.

Broo

Consideration of Lunar Days

In the S─Бrasaс╣Гgraha:[^FNB000127]

┬▓┬▓Dvit─лy─Б, Pa├▒cam─л and especially с╣вaс╣гс╣нh─л; it could be done also on Dv─Бda┼Ы─л or on Trayoda┼Ы─л.

And somewhere:

┬▓┬│Dvit─лy─Б, Pa├▒cam─л, Saptam─л, Da┼Ыam─л, Trayoda┼Ы─л and P┼лrс╣Зim─Б are recommended, as they fulfil all desires.

┬▓тБ┤Thus, initiation is recommended during a pure day in the waxing fortnight, during the [heliacal] rising of Venus and Jupiter, under a good ascendant and when the moon and stars are favourable.

During the rising of Venus and Jupiter: not during the time when they have set.

Exceptions

In the Rudray─Бmala:[^FNB000128]

┬▓тБ╡One should give mantra initiation in a holy place, during the eclipse of the sun or the moon or during the Strand or D─Бmana days, and not consider the month, lunar, mansion, and so on, ┬▓тБ╢for at that time there is always the strength of a good ascendant, the moon, the stars and so on. A mantra accepted there will increase oneтАЩs duration of life, wealth and offspring.

The Strand-day is the festival of offering the Pavitra-strand in ┼Ъr─Бvaс╣Зa; the D─Бmana day is the festival of offering Damanaka-flowers in Caitra. There: in a holy place and so on.

Broo

Elsewhere:[^FNB000129]

┬▓тБ╖Nothing is equal to the time of a solar eclipse: whatever is done then will all bear unlimited fruits. One should not consider month, lunar day, solar day and so on during a solar eclipse.

With this verse and a half, the author shows the excellence of a solar eclipse even compared to holy places and so on.

And in the Tattvas─Бgara:[^FNB000130]

┬▓тБ╕Since attaining even one meeting with true preceptors is rare, when one attains their consent, that is a great day for initiation, whether one is in a village, in the forest or in a field or whether it is day or night. ┬▓тБ╣When by fate the guru arrives, when initiation comes by his order, when there is the desireтАФthat is initiation, following the order of the guru. ┬│тБ░A holy place, a vow, a fire sacrifice, a bath or recitations are never the causes of initiationтАФit comes only when the true guru appears by his own will.

The author shows a further exception to all of these rules with the verse and a half beginning with тАЬwhen there is the desireтАЭ.

Rules for Constructing the Pavilion

┬│┬╣Initiation is of four types, divided into Ceremonial and so on. Among these, Ceremonial initiation will be described in an abbreviated way.

And so on: Dimensional, Vocalic and Penetrative. Also, in the ┼Ъ─Бrad─Бtilaka (4.3): тАЬIt is said to be fourfold as it is divided into Ceremonial and so on; Ceremonial, Vocalic, Dimensional and Penetrative.тАЭ[^FNB000131]

┬│┬▓After cleaning the ground and worshipping the divinity of the place in it, one should make a pavilion measuring seven cubits with a delightful sacrificial altar.

After cleaning: after preparing [the ground] by removing chaff, hair, coal, bones, gravel and other impurities. The rules for worshipping the divinity of the place are well-known and will be given below in connection with constructing a temple (20.85тАУ181) in accordance with books such as the ┼Ъ─Бrad─Бtilaka. Out of fear of prolixity, they are not given here. [тАж] Some want a pavilion measuring six, eight, twelve or sixteen cubits. As it is said in the Vasiс╣гс╣нha Saс╣Гhit─Б:[^FNB000132] тАЬтАж measuring six, eight, twelve or sixteen cubits on each sideтАЭ.[^FNB000133] In the middle of the pavilion one should fashion a delightful altar, one that is beautiful by not being too low, too high, too short or too long. As it is said:[^FNB000134] тАЬOne should construct a delightful altar in the middle, five cubits long, quadrangular and four-faced, raised by one cubit.тАЭ And in the Vasiс╣гс╣нha Saс╣Гhit─Б:[^FNB000135] тАЬOne should construct an altar for worship in the north-west or in the north-east, raised by one cubit and four cubits long on all sides.тАЭ The contradiction here should be avoided by recognising various opinions and various pavilions. The conclusion is that in consideration of the pavilion, one should fashion an excellent sacrificial altar in the middle.

┬│┬│It should have eight flags, four gates, arches made of milky trees and surrounded by a garland of Ku┼Ыa grass augmented by a threefold string.

The author further describes the pavilion in this verse. It should have eight flags in the eight directions, and it should have arches made of trees that have a milky sap, such as fig, that are sunk one cubit into the ground outside the gates. As it is said in the Matsya Pur─Бс╣Зa (264.15cdтАУ16ab): тАЬThe eastern gate should be made of Plakс╣гa; the southern, of Uс╕Нumbara; the western, of A┼Ыvattha; and the northern, of Nyagrodha.тАЭ[^FNB000136] [The pavilion] should be surrounded, enveloped on all sides with a garland of Ku┼Ыa grass augmented or joined with a string folded three times. Rules for Fashioning the Pit

┬│тБ┤On its northern side, the wise one should make a quadrangular pit with three girdles, measuring twenty-four digits.[^FNB000138]

Its: the pavilionтАЩs. The three girdles are ramparts fashioned according to the rules above the excavation, one over the other.

┬│тБ╡The excavation should be made to the measure of having an elevation of three girdles. Outside that excavation one should definitely make a collar of one digit.

One should make an excavation to the measure of twenty-four digits together with an elevation of three girdles measuring nine digits. The meaning is that one should not excavate all of the measure into the ground. As such, one should excavate fifteen digits underneath the three girdles. It should be understood that one will then arrive at the pit described, possessing a hollow of twenty-four digits when joined with the elevation of the three girdles. an elephantтАЩs lower lip, having a girdle raised by one digit and having a slit in the middle.

The connection between these two verses is that one should make a receptacle on the western side of the pit. It should be shaped like an elephantтАЩs lower lip: narrow at the top and broad at the base, like the leaf of the A┼Ыvattha tree. In the proper way: it should be turned towards the east. The meaning is that one should make a girdle of one digit around it, and the top of the vulva, which enters the middle of the pit, should be one digit [wide], and at the bottom of the vulva, two circular shapes like the frontal prominences on an elephant for the Arghya vessel. As it is said in the Vasiс╣гс╣нha Saс╣Гhit─Б:[^FNB000140] тАЬTo the north-east of the house the wise one should make a pavilion, measuring six, eight, twelve or sixteen cubits on each side, having four gates and decorated with arches and so on. One should have a quadrangular pit made in its middle: a quadrangular pit two spans[^FNB000141] and four digits deep for Br─Бhmaс╣Зas; [two spans and] three digits deep for Kс╣гatriyas; [two spans and] two digits deep for Vai┼Ыyas; and just a cubit for ┼Ъ┼лdras.[^FNB000142] The first girdle should be twelve digits wide and for digits high on all sides. On top of it should be a rampartтАФrampart means girdle[^FNB000143]тАФeight digits wide on all sides. On top of that, one should again make a third rampart four digits wide and similarly high, and in the middle of the western side a vulva facing east, six digits broad and twelve digits long, raised at the back as the lower lip of an elephant, having a cleft and raised in the middle. In a pit measuring one cubit there should be a collar measuring eight grains:[^FNB000144] those who desire the fruit of enjoyment or liberation should carefully make the collar, and a navel.[^FNB000145] Alternatively, the pit may have one girdle.тАЭ

┬│тБ╣For fifty oblations, the pit should measure a fist;[^FNB000146] for a hundred oblations, an elbow;[^FNB000147] for a thousand, a cubit;тАж

рд╣рд╕реНрдд178рдорд╛рддреНрд░рдВ рд╕реНрдердгреНрдбрд┐рд▓рдВ рд╡рд╛ рд╕рдВрдХреНрд╖рд┐рдкреНрддреЗ рд╣реЛрдордХрд░реНрдордгрд┐ реерекрекрее

Broo

тБ┤тБ░тАж for a hundred thousand, four cubits; for ten million, eight of them. The pit should be quadrangular and excavated in the same way.

Of them: of cubits. In the same way: the meaning is that one should excavate the pit to a depth that is the same as its length and breadth. It should also be understood to have an elevation of girdles as described before.

тБ┤┬╣One can offer more oblations in a pit for a lesser number, but not a lesser number in one for a great number.

In this verse the author again gives further specifics. More oblations, a greater number of oblations can be offered into a pit meant for a lesser number, for fewer oblations, since a smaller number is included in the greater.[^FNB000148] The meaning is that one should not offer a smaller number of oblations into a pit intended for a larger number. This has also been stated by the learned:[^FNB000149] тАЬA larger number is allowed in a pit meant for a smaller amount, but [that for] an unspecified pit or less is never desirable in a larger one.тАЭ

тБ┤┬▓The wise one should correctly and carefully construct the pit; otherwise many faults will arise, causing much suffering.

With this verse, the author writes about the merit of pit that follows the rules given and the fault in transgressing them.

This has been said by the T─Бntrikas:[^FNB000150]

тБ┤┬│A pit that has these characteristics awards oneтАЩs desired goal, but a pit that is for too few or too many [oblations] gives many faults. тБ┤тБ┤Therefore, one who desires welfare should construct it after careful consideration; or for simplified rituals of oblations, a heap measuring a cubit.

And by H─Бrita (тАУ):[^FNB000151]

тБ┤тБ╡When the length is too great or small oneтАЩs life is certainly shortened. When it is too deep, one becomes diseased; when too shallow, one loses oneтАЩs wealth. When the pit is bent there will be affliction; when the girdles are cut, death; тБ┤тБ╢when there are too few girdles, sorrow; when there are too many, oneтАЩs livestock will die. Without a receptacle, the wife will perish; without a collar, one loses oneтАЩs welfare.

[тАж]

And this is the measurement of a digit:

тБ┤тБ╖Eight of the broad parts of a grain of barley horizontally or three grains of rice vertically is known as the measure of a digit, the middle part of the middle finger.

тБ┤тБ╕The details for the production of the Sruc, Sruva and so on should be learnt from other books. Out of fear of prolixity they are not given here.

With regard to constructing the pit and so on the author gives the measure of a digit. [тАж] It is also said elsewhere: тАЬThose who know mantras say that eight grains of barley placed horizontally is a digit (aс╣Еgula); twelve digits is a span (t─Бla); and two spans is a cubit (hasta); two cubits is a handle (kiс╣гku); two of them is a bow-length (dhanus); a thousand of bow-lengths is a call (kro┼Ыa); two of them is called a pasture-length (gavy┼лti); and three of them the sages call an yoking-distance (yojana).тАЭ [тАж] The Sruc and Sruva are implements needed for libations. For the production of means the rules for fashioning them. Here, in the context of fashioning the pit, whatever other details are to be known, they also the wise ones should learn from books such as the Vasiс╣гс╣нha Saс╣Гhit─Б. They are not given here, in this book, for fear of proxility, fearing that the book will become too voluminous.

one cubit. One should first make a quadrangle measuring five or seven digits [square] respectively and then a hollow one third of that within, decorated with a circle inside. Having evenly carved out the hollow sidewise, lengthwise and downward, one should remove one fourth of a digit from its outside, and then half of the remainder from that onwards. With the remaining half of that, one should make a beautiful girdle by the hollow. One should make [a neck] one third as wide [as the quadrangle] and one or one and a half digits long; at its end should be a mouth four or five digits wide. Its middle and end should be two or three digits and very beautiful. In the area of the neck one should sink down a channel [wide] as the little finger. The rest should be made into a handle decorated according to taste.

The Sruva should measure one cubit and have a quadrangle. One should make a round cup[^FNB000153] measuring two digits; it should look beautiful as a cowтАЩs hoofprint on somewhat muddy ground. O sage, one should place the Sruc and Sruva on an unbroken and beautiful Pal─Б┼Ыa leaf (Butea Frondosa); or in the case of simplified fire rituals, on an A┼Ыvattha leaf (Ficus Religiosa).тАЭ[^FNB000154]

And in the ┼Ъ─Бrad─Бtilaka (3.94тАУ105ab): тАЬThe knower should make a Sruc in the following way. The wise one should cut a piece of ┼Ъr─лparс╣З─л- (Gmelina Arborea), ┼Ъiс╣Гс╣гapa- (Dalbergia Sissoo) or fig-tree wood, one cubit long and then divide it into 36 parts: twenty parts will be for the handle, eight for the altar, one for the neck and seven for the mouth. The width of the neck should be one third of that of the altar and the point [of the mouth] should be like the neck. One should fashion a passage in the mouth for the flow of clarified butter wide like the little finger. In the middle of the altar one should make a lotus, one part wide, and outside of that a hollow measuring one part. Its depth should be three parts and around should be a circle of half a part. One should fashion the petals around measuring one part, and there should be a girdle around the altar of half a measure.[^FNB000155] The water-jars at the bottom and the top of the handle should be three parts and four parts[^FNB000156] wide, respectively. The water-jars[^FNB000157] should have the length of two and four parts of the handle. Six parts of the bottom of the altar should have the shape of a tortoise. On

Rules for the Initiatory Maс╣Зс╕Нala

тБ┤тБ╣Now, once the pavilion has been sprinkled with the five products of the cow and with fragrant water, one should draw the Initiatory Maс╣Зс╕Нala on top of the altar according to the rules.

In the following three verses, the author describes the rules for the Maс╣Зс╕Нala. [тАж] According to the rules: following all that will be said below. On top of the altar: on the altar that has been erected inside the pavilion.

тБ╡тБ░In its middle, a lotus of eight petals; then around, three circles; then the Signs, then a seat with four legs; тБ╡┬╣beyond that, four terraces in the four directions, and then four gates, decorated with angles, ornaments and sub-ornaments.

The connection between these and the previous verse is that on should draw a lotus of eight petals in the middle of the diagram. [тАж] The Signs are the twelve signs of the zodiac beginning with Aries. [тАж] There should be ornaments everywhere besides the gates and on their sides sub-ornaments, and at the edges four anglesтАФthat is the meaning. And this is the arrangement: тАЬFirst, one should draw seventeen vertical lines, and then, on top of them, one should draw the same amount of horizontal lines with the same distances between them. In this way one will arrive at 256 squares, and once one has erased the sixteen squares in the middle, one should draw a lotus there surrounded by three circles. Outside of them, one should erase the [following] two rows of 48 squares and there draw the twelve signs of the zodiac.

Broo

There, in order to situate the signs, one should draw four lines from the east to the west and from the south to the north in between the three circles next to the edges of the petals of the lotus and the outer line connected to the seats. Outside of this, one should then erase the next row of 36 squares and fashion the seat and also feet of four [squares] at the corners. Outside of this, one should erase the next row of 44 squares and make four passages in the four directions. Outside of this, with the 112 squares on the last two rows one should make four gates and, on both sides, ornaments, then sub-ornaments and then four corners.тАЭ

There is also this method. тАЬThe four middle squares of the outer row and the two middle squares on the inner row make one gate of six squares. One square on the outer row next to the gate and three squares on the inner row make up one ornament of four squares. Next, three squares of the outer row and one square on the inner row make one sub-ornament of four squares. The remaining six squares make up the corner.тАЭ[^FNB000159] In this way one should understand the ornaments, sub-ornaments and corners on both sides. Following the same procedure in the three other directions one should fill up the rest of the 112 squares. This is the drift.

The Worship That Is a Part of Initiation

тБ╡┬▓After the preceptor has completed his morning rites, he should place the conch and the items for worship in their proper places, in accordance with what will be written later.

Broo

The author will now, in verses2.52тАУ79, show the rules for establishing the waterpot. After completing his morning rites: the daily duties of worshipping the Lord, from the morning bath to surrendering oneтАЩs very self. How? In accordance with what will be written later, that is, below. The meaning is that all the procedures will become evident when they will be given below, in the context of the main worship. One should understand similar cases elsewhere below in the same way. In their proper places means among other things that facing east, one should sit down on oneтАЩs own seat in front of the Maс╣Зс╕Нala, recite the Saс╣Еkalpa for initiation, perform Ny─Бsas such as M─Бtс╣Ыk─Б Ny─Бsa and then place to the left the items for worship and the liquids of Arghya and so on, poured into their respective vessels one after the other. On the right side on should place the flowers and so on. All of this will be explained in detail below, in the context of the main worship (5.29тАУ31).

First, the Procedure for Establishing the Waterpot

тБ╡┬│After worshipping the preceptors and Gaс╣Зe┼Ыa, one should worship the seat and then place down grains and Darbhas in the middle of the lotus.

One should worship the preceptors, oneтАЩs own preceptor, grand-preceptor, etc., as well as N─Бrada and previously perfected Bh─Бgavatas in the northern seat of the Maс╣Зс╕Нala, from the northwest to the northeast. One should worship them with sandalwood paste and so on, using their respective names in the dative case and adding

NAMAс╕д (obeisance) at the end, show the Praс╣З─Бma Mudr─Б and then accept their blessings. On should then worship Gaс╣Зe┼Ыa in the same way in the passage on the south side. After one has thus prayed for the removal of obstacles, one should worship the seat in the middle of the Maс╣Зс╕Нala, as will be described later, and then place down on the pericarp grains, that is, one ─Ас╕Нhaka[^FNB000160] of grain and one eight of that of white rice, and on top of that Darbhas. One should understand all of this to follow the statements of other books. Darbhas should be understood to refer to K┼лrcas, that is, three blades of Ku┼Ыa grass tied with a Brahma knot,[^FNB000161] together with Akс╣гata.[^FNB000162] Some say тАЬfistfuls of Ku┼ЫaтАЭ instead.

Correctly: Visualising the unity of the seat and the waterpot, one should fill the waterpot with clean sacred water alone, reciting the letters of the alphabet three times in backwards order, from

Kс╣вA to A, and the root mantra. And also, тАЬIf one is able, one can also fill it with camphor water, cow milk, the five products of the cow, herbal water, water infused with the sap of milky trees or water with some other great herbs.тАЭ The vowels are fourteen, but with their attendants Visarga and Anusv─Бra they are sixteen. Together with them, one should place the sixteen parts of the moon into the water of the pot, one after the other, and then worship them with flowers and so on.

And they are as follows:[^FNB000170]

Rules for Establishing the Conch

тБ╢┬╣One should pour the eight fragrances into a conch filled with clean water, invoke all these parts and then establish life in them, one after the other.

In this verse, the author shows the rules for filling the conch. тАЬFollowing the rulesтАЭ should be supplied here from the earlier verse (2.59). Hence, it should be understood that filled with clean water could also, as before, mean filled with camphor water and so on, if one is able [to procure such]. All these parts, the [38] parts of fire, the sun and the moon as given before, should be invoked one after the other, one by one, after which one should establish life in them. And the procedure for establishing life in all of them should be learned from other texts, such as the commentary on the Kramad─лpik─Б written by ┼Ъr─л Puruс╣гottama Vana.[^FNB000171]

тБ╖тБ╖Into this pitcher, the preceptor should invoke the highest light in the correct way, create the parts and then worship it by offering a seat and so on.

Creating the parts is as follows:[^FNB000178]

тБ╖тБ╕Creating the parts means doing Ny─Бsa of the six limbs on the limbs of the divinity.

тБ╖тБ╣But some say that creating the parts is creating a body for its light by all the Ny─Бsas, except for the Ny─Бsa of the hands and the P─лс╣нha Ny─Бsa.[^FNB000179]

What do they say? That he explains with creating and so on. Creating a body means by meditation fashioning a form for its light, the light having the essence of Brahman.

тБ╕тБ░One should now, according to the rules given below, worship this Lord in the waterpot, together with his limbs, secondary limbs and his coverings, up to the offering of food.

This Lord: ┼Ъr─л Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa, the highest Brahman in a human form. Now, one should worship him by invoking him and so on, up to the offering of eatables. How? According to the method given below, in its primary place, in the context of the daily worship. Hence, there only all the different procedures will be given at length; having seen them there, one should do the same kind of worship here as well. The meaning is that what has been written now is sufficient.[^FNB000180]

тБ╕┬╣After offering foodstuffs, one should place beautiful lamps made of flour, having seeds and sprouts, all around the Maс╣Зс╕Нala.

Around the Maс╣Зс╕Нala one should place the best lamps, nicely burning with cow ghee and having cups with seeds and sprouts. Made of flour means that their cups are made of barley or some other flour.

proper way. тБ╕┬│Having scattered mustard seeds and sprinkled the five products of the cow there, he should worship the V─Бstupuruс╣гa[^FNB000181] in the middle, and in the directions, their lords.

In verses82тАУ97, the author describes the rules for the initiatory fire sacrifice. The mustard seeds should have the Astra mantra[^FNB000184] recited over them. There refers to the pit. Their lords are the lords of the ten directions.

тБ╕тБ┤Having performed the acts of drying and so forth, and after sprinkling the firepit with Ku┼Ыa water and scrubbing it, one should draw a Maс╣Зс╕Нala in it with a vulva[^FNB000185] and so on.

And so on refers to Akс╣гata and K┼лrcas.

тБ╣┬│Then, having enclosed the fire[^FNB000196] and purified the ghee in the correct way, one should after that sacrifice with the Vy─Бhс╣Ыtis[^FNB000197] and then again three times. тБ╣тБ┤Then one should perform for it the sacraments in the correct order, beginning with impregnation and ending with marriage, with the correct mantra and eight libations.

One should enclose the fire with Ku┼Ыa blades and so on. The words in the correct way applies to everything here. The methods for purifying the ghee and so on by Heating, Illuminating,[^FNB000198] etc., are well known to sacrificial experts. If they are required, they should be learnt from the commentary on the Kramad─лpik─Б by ┼Ъr─л Puruс╣гottama Vana. After that, having in the correct way sacrificed with

Oс╣В and the Vy─Бhс╣Ыtis, one should again offer three libations with the root mantra of fire, the Vai┼Ыv─Бnara mantra. One should then perform the sacraments for this fire, one after the other, with eight libations each and the scriptural mantra that begins with

Oс╣В and ends with

SV─АH─А and with another mantra appropriate for the particular ritual in question. The rules for all of these rituals as well should be specifically learnt from their respective books.

тБ╣тБ╡When the fire has been sanctified in this manner and one has worshipped the, one should invoke the Lord there and properly worship him, beginning with sandalwood paste and ending with a light.

There refers to this seat. The meaning is that one should worship in a way that begins with the offering of sandalwood paste and ends with the offering of a light. And the worship that ends with the light is in regard to the food offerings to the tongues of the fire that follow.[^FNB000199] The specifics of worshipping the seat and invoking the Lord will be given below (6.14тАУ31).

тБ╣тБ╢Having visualised the fire as the tongue of the Lord, the wise one should offer one thousand and one hundred and eight libations of rice boiled in milk with sugar and ghee.

[тАж]

тБ╣тБ╖After these libations, the practitioner should now according to the rules sacrifice with ghee to the great Vy─Бhс╣Ыtis, and then in the correct way offer tribute to the planet, the star, the Karaс╣Зa[^FNB000200] and so on.

Now, after this, once the practitioner has offered ghee to the great Vy─Бhс╣Ыtis according to the rules, following the procedure described in the scriptures. His being a practitioner also implies things such sprinkling himself and the disciple with offered water and preparing a Tilaka of sacrificial ashes after finishing the fire sacrifice.

In the correct way: at the places of the Astrological signs within the Maс╣Зс╕Нala he should offer tribute to the planet and so on with a third part of the sweet pudding that is left over after the sacrifice, one after the other and with their respective mantras. The particular rules for this should also be learnt from the same book. And so on implies that one should offer tribute to the Lion, Tiger, Boar, Donkey, Elephant, Bull and so on in between Pisces and Aries.[^FNB000201] Then it should be understood that with a fourth part, one should in a place smeared with cow dung to the south of the Maс╣Зс╕Нala one should give tribute to the fire, to the regent of light and to all the associates of Viс╣гс╣Зu. And in all the cases there, when offering water, sandalwood paste, flowers and so on, one should use the respective mantra ending with

NAMAс╕д. When offering tribute, one should end with

SV─АH─А, but it should be understood that when one then again offers water, one should end with

Tс╣ЪPYAT─АM (may

Broo

Measures for the Ingredients for the Fire Offerings

тБ╣тБ╕For an offering into the fire, one needs one ┼Ъukti of milk, one Karс╣гa of ghee, and the same amount of the five products of the cowтАФso say the thoughtful ones. тБ╣тБ╣The same amount of rice cooked with milk and honey is called an Akс╣гa. There should be one Prasс╣Ыti of sour milk and one handful of parched rice. And so on.[^FNB000202]

┬╣тБ░тБ░Now, after bowing down, one should offer drinking water and ─Аcamana and then perform the worship up to the offering of the self, proceeding according to the rules to be given.

Now, after the offerings of tribute, one should offer obeisance, purified water for drinking and after that water for ─Аcamana. The procedure for all of this as well will be considered in the context of the daily worship where it will be expanded on. One should offer all the other rituals that follow that of offering water, beginning with giving a part of the sacrificial food to Viс╣гvaksena and offering the Lord water for washing the mouth and so on and ending with offering oneтАЩs own self. This also should follow the procedures to be given in the context of the daily worship. This is the meaning.

Rules for Guru and Disciple

┬╣тБ░┬╣In the correct way, the disciple, following the vow and controlling his speech, should now be led in. One should place down the letters and their parts on his body and then instruct him about them.

Now, after this, the older disciples should lead in the disciple, who is fasting and observing silence. In the correct way means that he should be made to bow down, be sprinkled with water for sprinkling and the Astra mantra,[^FNB000203] made to eat some five products of the cow, after which the guru should place down the letters and their parts on his body, teach him the [Ny─Бsa of the] letters and the meditations that go with them.

Broo

┬╣тБ░┬▓Remembering the Lord along with his covering in the pitcher, the guru should recite the mantra a thousand and eight times, eat something and lie down.

The words in the correct way should be supplied. Now, thinking about the Lord along with his covering inside the pitcher into which he has been established, [the guru] should touch the water of the pitcher, recite the mantra a thousand and eight times, offer flowers in his cupped hands, recite prayers, eat a little of the five products of the cow, etc., and then lie down on a clean bed, deliberating on the ritual texts connected to initiation and so on. This is the meaning.

┬╣тБ░┬│Resting on an antelope skin on top of Ku┼Ыa grass, the disciple should remember the letters and the guru. Following his vow, he should lie down and recite the letters until falling asleep.

After the disciple has been given the instructions pertaining to the letters, he sits down on the skin of a black antelope on top of Ku┼Ыa grass and meditates on the letters and the guru. Remaining fasting and keeping his head towards the east or the north, he should then lie down reciting the letters until falling asleep.

These Were the Duties of the Preceding Day. Now the Duties of the Day of Initiation

┬╣тБ░тБ┤After completing the morning duties, the preceptor should worship the pitcher as before. Having offered oblations into the fire and given tribute, he should perform the rituals up to the offering of the self.

After finishing all the morning duties from the morning bath to offering the self, [the guru] should worship the Lord in the pitcher as before, then perform the fire sacrifice. Having offered tribute, he should perform all the other rituals again, such as offering drinking water up to the offering of the self directed to the pitcher. This is the meaning.

┬╣тБ░тБ╡Showing the Saс╣Гh─Бra Mudr─Б, he should join the attendant divinities to Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa, and then, meditating on him as consisting of nectar, he should merge him as well as the fire into himself.

Broo

Imagining the attendant divinities, except for the preceptor and Gaс╣Зe┼Ыa,[^FNB000204] as merged into the Lord by uniting them with him by the ritual of retraction, he should meditate on him, God, as consisting of nectar, as being established in a form of undivided, complete bliss, and merge him, think of him as being dissolved.

┬╣тБ░тБ╢The indwelling divinities of the flags, gates, directions, pitcher and the pavilion and so on should all be imagined as being forms of consciousness, united with the pitcher and worshipped.

[тАж] And so on refers to the indwelling divinities of the Maс╣Зс╕Нala, the sacrificial pit and so on.

┬╣тБ░тБ╖Then, after in the proper way retracting the preceptor, Gaс╣Зe┼Ыa and Viс╣гvaksena, he should touch the pitcher and recite the mantra a hundred and eight times.

In the proper way: after retracting the preceptor on to his head and worshipping him, he should also retract Gaс╣Зe┼Ыa into space and worship him, and then with the remaining ingredients after the fire sacrifice worship Viс╣гvaksena and retract him into space. This is the meaning.

┬╣тБ░тБ╕Now the fasting disciple should perform his morning duties. Nicely adorned and dressed in white cloth, he should please the Br─Бhmaс╣Зas with gifts.

He should perform his morning duties, that is the mandatory rituals such as bathing, before dressing in white cloth and adorning himself with beautiful ornaments for the sake of initiation. He should then please the Br─Бhmaс╣Зas who performed the rituals of the fire sacrifice with gifts of cows, land, cloth, grain and so on.

┬╣тБ░тБ╣Regarding the preceptor as the Lord, he should circumambulate him and bow down to him. He should give him the prescribed donation and then dedicate his own body to him.

Broo

As is also said in the Tenth Canto (BhP 10.80.41):[^FNB000205]

┬╣┬╣тБ░For this much true disciples should do for the sake of the preceptor: to give themselves and all their belongings to the preceptor with a pure mind.

[тАж]

Rules for the Anointment

┬╣┬╣┬╣One should make the disciple sit down on a seat in a bathing pavilion to the north of the sacrificial area and then performing the Drying up and so on on him.

In verses2.111тАУ116, the author describes the duties of the preceptor. [тАж] Here the following procedure should be considered. Having drawn lotuses, svastikas and other auspicious symbols in a solitary pavilion smeared with cow dung and decorated with a canopy and so on, he should establish a seat there and invite the disciple to sit on it, facing east. Having sat down facing the disciple, he should then perform the rituals of Bh┼лta┼Ыuddhi for him, that is, Drying, Burning, Flooding and so on (5.65тАУ73).

┬╣┬╣┬▓Having performed all the Ny─Бsas on the body of the disciple, beginning with M─Бtс╣Ыk─Б Ny─Бsa and ending with P─лс╣нha Ny─Бsa, he should worship him with the P─лс╣нha mantra.[^FNB000206]

He should worship him, the Lord that he has directed into this body, by offering flowers in his cupped hands. This is the meaning.

┬╣┬╣┬│Having placed Gorocan─Б[^FNB000207] together with Ku┼Ыa grass and flowers on the head of the disciple, he should bring the pitcher to his side to the accompaniment of music and so on.

Broo

[тАж]. Some say that he should make a Tilaka with the Gorocan─Б. With the help of trusted saintly persons he should bring the pitcher, the waterpot that has been sanctified earlier on, to the side of the disciple. And so on refers to the blessings of Br─Бhmaс╣Зas, auspicious sounds, songs, chanting and so on.

┬╣┬╣тБ┤Now, after praying to blessed Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa, the preceptor should do N─лr─Бjana[^FNB000208] of the disciple with the cloth from the pitcher and then place the flowers and so on from it on his head.

Now, after this, the guru should pray: тАЬO Lord! Make yourself especially present in my mind and be pleased to give this child of saintly qualities your blessing.тАЭ[^FNB000209] Himself facing the north, he should hold the pitcher in his left hand and do N─лr─Бjana of the disciple with the cloth covering the opening of the pitcher. He should then place the flowers and so on that covered the pitcher on the head of the disciple. These are the rules to be considered in this regard.

As it is said:[^FNB000210]

┬╣┬╣тБ╡Having taken hold of the pitcher in the correct way, he should place the flowers from its top on the head of the disciple and recite the M─Бtс╣Ыk─Бs in his mind.

The author demonstrates these rules with the present verse. The flowers refer to the A┼Ыvattha blossoms placed on top of the pitcher.

┬╣┬╣тБ╢Then he should sprinkle the disciple three times with the root mantra. Accompanied by the blessings of Br─Бhmaс╣Зas and auspicious sounds, he should then ceremonially bathe him with water from the pitcher reciting the mantras.

He should first sprinkle him three times with the root mantra and then, grasping the pitcher with both hands, bathe the head of the disciple with its water, so that it covers all of his body. This is the meaning. [тАж]

The Mantra of Ceremonial Bathing

In the Vasiс╣гс╣нha Saс╣Гhit─Б:[^FNB000211]

┬╣┬╣тБ╖May the gods bathe you: Brahm─Б, Viс╣гс╣Зu and Mahe┼Ыvara! May V─Бsudeva, master of the world, may mighty Saс╣Гkarс╣гaс╣Зa, Pradyumna and Aniruddha confer might to you. ┬╣┬╣тБ╕May the ten guardians of the directions always protect you: Indra, Agni, Viс╣гс╣Зu, Yama, Nirс╣Ыti, Varuс╣Зa, V─Бyu, Kubera, ┼Ъiva, Brahm─Б. ┬╣┬╣тБ╣K─лrti, Lakс╣гm─л, Dhс╣Ыti, Medh─Б, Puс╣гс╣нi, ┼Ъraddh─Б, Kriy─Б, Mati, Buddhi, Lajj─Б, Vapu, ┼Ъ─Бnti, M─Бy─Б, Nidr─Б and Bh─Бvan─Б[^FNB000212]тАФ┬╣┬▓тБ░may they bathe you! R─Бhu, Ketu and the revered gods, D─Бnavas, Gandharvas, Yakс╣гas, R─Бkс╣гasas, serpents, ┬╣┬▓┬╣с╣Ъс╣гis, sages, cows, divine mothers, wives of the gods, Dhruva, N─Бgas, Daityas and Apsarasas, ┬╣┬▓┬▓divine arrows and all the divine swords, the kings, carriers, herbs, jewels, K─Бlakeyas, ┬╣┬▓┬│rivers, oceans, mountains, holy places and streams of waterтАФmay they bathe you for the attainment of all of your desired goals.

[тАж]

Rules for Imparting the Mantra

┬╣┬▓тБ┤Dressed in two cloths, the disciple should do ─Аcamana within the sacrificial pavilion, go to the preceptor, bow down to him with devotion and then sit down on the right side of the guru.

Dressed in two cloths means wearing new white cloth, not touching the bathing cloth and having done ─Аcamana. He should bow down with devotion: the meaning is that thinking of him as God, he should repeatedly bow down with the eight parts of his body, grasping his feet. With folded hands and fixing his mind on him, he should sit down on the right side of the preceptor but facing him, while the preceptor sits facing east, having completed his Pr─Бс╣З─Бy─Бma, sixfold Ny─Бsa and so on.

┬╣┬▓тБ╡He should present sandalwood and so on to the preceptor, offer as much rice pudding as a person would eat to Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa, and then offer flowers in his cupped hands.

And so on refers to flowers, incense and so forth.

┬╣┬▓тБ╢With the help of Ny─Бsas such as that of the five limbs, he should then make over him, the child, decorated with the seals and so on of the tradition and folding his hands, to blessed Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa.

He should make over or offer him, the disciple, to blessed Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa. The word child implies an affectionate relation, that the disciple is now his child. He should be decorated with things such as seals, Tilaka and garlands of the tradition, that have been established by preceptorial succession, as well as golden finger-rings and so on.

┬╣┬▓тБ╖Touching the palm of his hand to his head, he should utter the mantra three times into his right ear in the correct way together with its seer and so on, ┬╣┬▓тБ╕but a long mantra should be recited until the disciple grasps it. Meditating on the unity between preceptor, divinity and mantra, the disciple should then recite it.

has appeared in the body of the disciple, who has opened his eyes, the preceptor should decorate him with sandalwood paste and so on, worship him with five articles and at an auspicious time, accompanied by the auspicious sounds of singing and instruments, place his palm on the head of the disciple, instruct him in the seer, metre, divinity and so on, and then utter the root mantra three times in his right ear.

Until the disciple grasps it means that he should recite it as many times as needed until the mantra becomes fixed. [тАж]

┬╣┬▓тБ╣Placing Akс╣гata and water into the right hand of the disciple, the preceptor should say this mantra: тАЬMay it be the same for us!тАЭ.

He should say: тАЬFrom now on, may this mantra be the same, may it give the same fruit for me and for you.тАЭ

┬╣┬│┬╣The preceptor should give the Mah─Бpras─Бda rice pudding to the disciple and place Akс╣гata on his head, praying for his welfare. ┬╣┬│┬▓Having received the mantra by the grace of the preceptor, the disciple should recite it a hundred and eight times and then hear the regulations.

He should give the disciple the personтАЩs portion of rice pudding that had been offered to the Lord and that now is Mah─Бpras─Бda.[^FNB000214] Praying for his welfare means statements such as тАЬLife, health, majesty, unceasing victory itself, welfare and again lifeтАФmay you always enjoy themтАЭ. Having recited, repeated the mantra, he should then hear from the preceptor the regulations, the customs of Ny─Бsa, meditation and so on, as also other Vaiс╣гс╣Зava rules.

The Regulations

In the N─Бrada Pa├▒car─Бtra (16.301, 307cdтАУ308ab, 311cdтАУ312ab, 322, 324тАУ325, 326cdтАУ328ab):[^FNB000215]

┬╣┬│┬│One should not teach others oneтАЩs mantra or utter it publicly; likewise, one should keep the scripture secret and protect it likes oneтАЩs own body. ┬╣┬│тБ┤One should have the highest devotion for the Vaiс╣гс╣Зavas and especially for the preceptors and one should perform worship as one is able and care for the unfortunate.

The scripture refers to texts such as the blessed Bh─Бgavata or else to those connected to worship. The unfortunate means saints who have fallen into misfortune.

┬╣┬│тБ╡One should humbly carry on oneтАЩs head that which has come from the house of Viс╣гс╣Зu and then place it into water; one should not throw it away just anywhere.

That which has come: offered flowers and so on. As it is said in the same book, in connection to expiation (25.39): тАЬHe who throws away something offered to Viс╣гс╣Зu just anywhere or gives it to an undeserving person should do a hundred and one recitations.тАЭ

┬╣┬│тБ╢One should consider Lord Viс╣гс╣Зu to reside in the sun and the moon, in cows, the A┼Ыvattha tree, fire, the preceptor and the Br─Бhmaс╣Зas. ┬╣┬│тБ╖One should never stay in a place where one hears jealous censure of the preceptor but depart, remembering Hari. ┬╣┬│тБ╕O N─Бrada, one should never stay or talk with those who slander the preceptor, the Lord or scripture.

[тАж]

┬╣┬│тБ╣One should repeatedly remember oneтАЩs mantra in the morning, while doing circumambulations, when setting out, when away from home and especially when giving gifts. ┬╣тБ┤тБ░If one unexpectedly sees something wonderful and very exciting either in a dream or before oneтАЩs very eyes, one should not tell it to anyone except for the preceptor.

In another Pa├▒car─Бtra:[^FNB000216]

┬╣тБ┤┬╣I will now briefly tell you the regulations of the Pa├▒car─Бtrakas! Do not eat fish, meat, tortoise or pork.

Even though fish and meat are forbidden (2.165), tortoise and so on is further forbidden to prohibit the eating of [such kinds of meat] even for those who sometimes eat meat because of illness or some other such reason.

┬╣тБ┤┬▓Do not eat off a brass plate or off Plakс╣гa- or Vaс╣нa-leaves. Do not spit in the temple and also avoid sneezing there. Never go inside with shoes on your feet.

The words тАЬin the templeтАЭ should be supplied in the latter cases here as well. Inside therefore means inside the temple. [тАж] Never can also mean nowhere inside the temple.

┬╣тБ┤┬│Do not eat on the Ek─Бda┼Ы─л of either fortnight; keep vigil during the night and perform special worship of the Lord.

Special: since Ek─Бda┼Ы─л is different from other lunar days, one should especially at that time worship by keeping awake. This is the meaning.

And in the Sammohana Tantra:

┬╣тБ┤тБ┤Keep your chosen deity secret, keep your preceptor secret, keep your mantra secret, keep your rosary secret!

┬╣тБ┤тБ╡Some hold that initiation occurs only when the disciple before the preceptor agrees to one hundred and four regulations.

In this verse, the author describes another opinion as to hearing the regulations. [тАж]

Broo

As it is said in the Viс╣гс╣Зu Y─Бmala:[^FNB000217]

┬╣тБ┤тБ╢The preceptor should diligently observe the disciple for a year. Then he should have him hear the one hundred and four rules, both injunctions and prohibitions:

[тАж]

┬╣тБ┤тБ╖Arising at the watch of Brahman; waking up great Viс╣гс╣Зu; doing his N─лr─Бjana with music; the morning bath according to the rules;тАж

Here the author first gives the fifty-two injunctions, beginning with arising at the watch of Brahman and ending with remembrance [at 2.162].

┬╣тБ┤тБ╕Dressing in two pure and new cloths; worship of the Lord; always wearing vertical Tilaka made of Gop─лcandana mud;тАж

[тАж] The meaning of another reading of the first line is that one should dress in two cloths brought by a pure person.[^FNB000218] Worship of the Lord refers to worship of the chosen Lord in water by oblations and so on. This is the meaning also of the other reading.[^FNB000219]

┬╣тБ┤тБ╣Wearing the five weapons; honouring the foot-nectar; wearing ornaments such as Tulas─л or pearl necklaces daily; ┬╣тБ╡тБ░removing the flowers offered to Viс╣гс╣Зu; smearing oneself with his sandalwood paste; devotedly worshiping the ┼Ъ─Бlagr─Бma stone or images; eating offered Tulas─л; picking Tulas─л according to the rules;тАж

Worship of the ┼Ъ─Бlagr─Бma stone or images is one injunction. [тАж] Instead of eating offered Tulas─л another reading is тАЬdecorating withтАЭ. The meaning is to wear offered Tulas─л as ornaments on the head and so on. [тАж]

┬╣тБ╡┬╣Performing Tantric Sandhy─Б in the proper way; tying the tuft of hair for the sake of rituals; offering oblations to the forefathers with water from the feet of Viс╣гс╣Зu; worshipping Hari with royal items, if able;тАж

If able means if one has the means. That is also the meaning of the reading тАЬaccording to ability.тАЭ The same applies to cases below as well [e.g., 2.160].

┬╣тБ╡┬▓Performing the mandatory and occasional rituals in a way that does not conflict with devotion to Viс╣гс╣Зu; performing the rites of Bh┼лta┼Ыuddhi, etc, and all the Ny─Бsas according to the rules;тАж

[In a way that does not conflict with the devotion to Viс╣гс╣Зu] means performing those rituals that are not in conflict with devotion to Viс╣гс╣Зu. The other reading is clear.[^FNB000220]

┬╣тБ╡┬│Devotedly offering fresh fruits and flowers; regular worship of Tulas─л; worship of the blessed Bh─Бgavata; ┬╣тБ╡тБ┤worship of Viс╣гс╣Зu at the three times of the day; daily hearing the Pur─Бс╣Зas; wearing clothes and other items that have been offered to Viс╣гс╣Зu;тАж

Hearing the Pur─Бс╣Зas means listening to texts such as the blessed Bh─Бgavata.

┬╣тБ╡тБ╡Performing all good deeds seeing the Master; honoring the orders of the preceptor; keeping faith in the words of the preceptor;тАж

Seeing the Master means considering the order of the Lord, or thinking, тАЬAs I am directed, so I shall act.тАЭ Or else it means, thinking тАЬmy MasterтАЭ, that is, having the mood of a servant.

┬╣тБ╡тБ╢Producing the Mudr─Бs of oneтАЩs own; devoted song; dance; producing the auspicious sounds of the conch and so on; showing the signs of the play of Hari; performing the daily fire sacrifice; offering tribute in the correct way;тАж

Producing the Mudr─Бs of oneтАЩs own: affixing such Mudr─Бs as are conformable to the divinity of oneтАЩs mantra. The meaning of the reading тАЬand of oneтАЩs ownтАЭ is also the same.

Broo

┬╣тБ╡тБ╖Welcoming and worshipping the saints; eating the remains of offerings; partaking of the leavings of betelnut; keeping the company of Vaiс╣гс╣Зavas; ┬╣тБ╡тБ╕enquiring about the particular Dharma; restrictedly and contentedly observing the three-day vow of Da┼Ыam─л and so on; being satisfied with whatever comes; ┬╣тБ╡тБ╣observing the Parvas, the festivals and so on; following the Eight Days; worshipping Viс╣гс╣Зu in all the seasons and with regal items,тАж

Welcoming and worshipping is one observation. The particular Dharma means that one should enquire about the duties of Vaiс╣гс╣Зavas, or else it means enquiring about the particular Dharma of the Lord. Restrictedly and contently observing the three day vow of Da┼Ыam─л and so on means to keep the vow of Da┼Ыam─л, Ek─Бda┼Ы─л and Dv─Бda┼Ы─л faithfully and following the rules for eating and so on. The Parva refers to Janm─Бс╣гс╣нam─л and so on, the festivals to visiting temples and so on; and so on refers to the particular rules for maintaining Tulas─л and flower gardens. The Eight Days are the eight Mah─Бdv─Бda┼Ы─лs; to follow them means to show them proper regard, that is, to observe them according to the rules. Worship in all the seasons means serving [the Lord] with various fruits and other items that are seasonal to spring and so on, or else it refers to rituals such swinging the Lord on a swing. If one is able, one should perform these rites with regal items. That is the meaning.

┬╣тБ╢тБ░Observing all the Vaiс╣гс╣Зava vows; considering the preceptor as God; regularly gathering Tulas─л; ┬╣тБ╢┬╣offering a bed and so on; and thinking about R─Бma, Skanda and others.

And so on refers to acts such as massaging the feet. [тАж] Thinking about R─Бma and others refers to statements such as тАЬOne who while lying down remembers R─Бma, Skanda, Hanum─Бn, Garuс╕Нa and Bh─лma ….тАЭ[^FNB000221]

┬╣тБ╢┬▓Not sleeping at the junctions of the day; not to bathe without mud; not to do ─Аcamana while standing; also sitting on the seat of the preceptor;тАж

Beginning with not sleeping and ending with Pras─Бda of Viс╣гс╣Зu [at 2.176], the author now lists the fifty-two prohibitions. The word also means nor indeed; it should be supplied everywhere below as well.

By mistake means even by mistake.

┬╣тБ╖┬│Bowing down with only one hand and so on; seeing the Master at the improper time; offering food and other items that are stale or bad in some other way;тАж

And so on means doing only one round of circumambulation and so on. All of this will be described and explained in detail in the proper context below (8.359тАУ364, 389тАУ394). Nevertheless, something is shown here as well for ease of understanding.

┬╣тБ╖тБ┤Reciting mantras without keeping count; revealing the mantra; regularly to give up primary times, even though able; to make use of secondary times;тАж

[тАж] In the case of the reading kad─Бsakty─Б the meaning is to give up the primary time because of attachment to despicable actions and the like. To make use of secondary times is a separate observation.[^FNB000230]

┬╣тБ╖тБ╡And not to accept the Pras─Бda of Viс╣гс╣ЗuтАФa Vaiс╣гс╣Зava should always avoid these. The preceptor should explain these one hundred and four prescriptions and prohibitions, ┬╣тБ╖тБ╢and after the disciple has accepted them by saying, тАЬso be itтАЭ, he should do N─лr─Бjana of him, have him worship the Lord and then recite the mantra into his right ear.

[тАж]

┬╣тБ╖тБ╖Then the disciple should get up with a satisfied heart and prostrate to the preceptor like a stick. He should place his lotus feet on his own head.

He should place or hold his, the guruтАЩs, lotus feet on his head with devotion for a long time.

maintain his own power unbroken. ┬╣тБ╖тБ╣The disciple should give the pitcher and all the other items, as well as other things according to his means, to the preceptor, bow down to him, worship the Br─Бhmaс╣Зas and feed them.

He should recite the mantra, the mantra that he has imparted, a thousand and eight times to maintain his own power unbroken or contained, that is, to safeguard his own strength. The pitcher and all the other items refer to the items brought for the sake of the initiation and placed in the pavilion. As well as other things refers to the gift for the mantra and so on. As it is said: тАЬTaking recourse to another mode,[^FNB000231] he should carefully please the preceptor. With gold and similar items he should please the wife and children of the preceptor.тАЭ According to his ability, he should also properly worship the Br─Бhmaс╣Зas, the officiating priests and also other true Br─Бhmaс╣Зas.

┬╣тБ╕тБ░Strenghtened by the blessings of the blessed preceptor and the Br─Бhmaс╣Зas, he should bid farewell to the preceptor and the others and eat together with his kinsmen.

┬╣тБ╕┬╣One who receives a mantra from a preceptor according to these rules is fortunate: he will live a long life and attain all of his goals.[^FNB000232]

Strengthened means completely developed. [тАж]

As it said in the conversation between ┼Ъr─л ┼Ъiva and Um─Б in the Sammohana Tantra:

┬╣тБ╕тБ╕One should properly sacrifice to the Lord on every Dv─Бda┼Ы─л but especially on a pure Dv─Бda┼Ы─л in the month of K─Бrttika, ┬╣тБ╕тБ╣fortunate one, on a Saс╣Еkr─Бnti or on a lunar or solar eclipse. Auspicious one, one who sees Lord Hari worshipped by the preceptor immediately attains satisfaction and all of his sins are destroyed.

The author explains the time for initiation in a verse and a half beginning with тАЬOne should тАжтАЭ. Pure means during the bright fortnight. Every Dv─Бda┼Ы─л means on the Dv─Бda┼Ы─лs during the bright fortnights of M─Бrga┼Ы─лrс╣гa, M─Бgha, ┼Ъr─Бvana and A┼Ыvina, in accordance with the statements of other books. On Saс╣Еkr─Бnti means on a Saс╣Еkr─Бnti during these particular months. Similar cases later on should be understood in the same way.

┬╣тБ╣тБ░Without a doubt he becomes equal to the gods. ┬╣тБ╣┬╣For a year the preceptor should observe Br─Бhmaс╣Зas, Kс╣гatriyas, Vai┼Ыyas and ┼Ъ┼лdras with regard to their birth, cleanliness, actions and so on.

Equal to the gods means equal to Brahm─Б and the others. In the following verse and a half he describes those who have the eligibility for initiation. Even in the reading bhakt─Бn─Бm, that word refers to servants, that is, ┼Ъ┼лdras.[^FNB000235]

┬╣тБ╣┬▓Having come to know those that have come to him, he should deliberate in his heart. And they, devotedly understanding him as the highest Lord of the self, should unceasingly devote themselves to the guru for a year, as if to Viс╣гс╣Зu.

When a year has passed, he will have come to know the birth and so on of those that have come to him, those who have come to his proximity. He should then in his mind deliberate as to whether they are suitable for initiation or not. Or else, as they have lived together in close proximity, he has come to know them by observing their conduct and so on. He should then deliberate in his heart or understanding, that is, ascertain their suitability for initiation. Or again, those who have come to him refer to who have surrendered unto him; in this case, the meaning is that he should know with certainty that they are eligible for initiation. This is the meaning also of the reading upapann─Бn.

┬▓тБ░тБ╕Having in this way properly worshipped Jan─Бrdana, God of gods, one should also in the correct way place the eight pitchers in the directions of the Maс╣Зс╕Нala, as well as fashion the ninth pitcher there, that of Viс╣гс╣Зu.

Properly worshipped means worshipped according to what has been described, and that should be gleaned from books such as the Kramad─лpik─Б.

┬▓тБ░тБ╣Those who desire liberation should be bathed with the pot of Viс╣гс╣Зu; those who desire prosperity should similarly be bathed with the pot of Indra. ┬▓┬╣тБ░Those who desire the majesty of victory should be bathed with that of Agni; the procedure of overcoming death is bathing with that of Yama. ┬▓┬╣┬╣For the destruction of evils, that of Nairс╣Ыti is mandated; for peace, one should bathe with that of Varuс╣Зa; for destruction of sin, with that of V─Бyu. ┬▓┬╣┬▓For one who wants riches, that of Kubera is mandated; to attain knowledge, that of Rudra. These are the pots of the protectors of the directions.

Then, after one has worshipped the Lord as well as Indra and the others with all the items of incense, lights and so on, one should show the Maс╣Зс╕Нala to the disciple. After he has offered flowers in his cupped hands, he should be made to bow down. Then it is to be understood that the disciple should be bathed with the nine pitchers of Viс╣гс╣Зu and so on. These verses describe the different results accruing from the different pitchers.

┬▓┬╣┬│The man who is bathed with even one is freed from all sins; he attains unimpeded knowledge and becomes a man always endowed with fortune. ┬▓┬╣тБ┤How much more does a man bathed with all nine become freed from sins! He becomes immediately similar to Viс╣гс╣Зu, or else a king.

In these two verses, the author further shows the special result of bathing with each one and then the great result of all of them together.

┬▓┬╣тБ╡Alternatively, one should worship the protectors of the directions properly and in the right order, in all the directions, with their respective names and with their six parts.

Broo

In this verse, the author provides an alternative for the worship. One should do worship with their respective names, with mantras consisting of their respective names, such as Indra, and of their six parts, that is, the six limbs beginning with the heart, one after the other.[^FNB000244]

┬▓┬╣тБ╢Now, after the gods that protect the directions have been worshipped, with a calm mind the preceptor should lead in the blindfolded disciples, ┬▓┬╣тБ╖burned by the syllable of fire, checked by the wind and nourished by the moon. The wise one should then make them hear the regulations.

Now the disciple, clothed in new white cloth and a similar upper cloth, decorated and blindfolded with a white cloth, should do ─Аcamana, circumambulate the Maс╣Зс╕Нala clockwise and be made to enter. [The preceptor] should do Bh┼лta┼Ыuddhi on him, seated as he is, facing the north, with the V─Бyu, Agni and Varuс╣Зa[^FNB000245] seeds. Then with folded hands and bent head he should be made to hear the regulations. This is the meaning of the two verses.

In the statement burned by the syllable of fire it should be understood that one conceives of oneself as being burned in meditation. The same applies below as well.

┬▓┬╣тБ╕One should not slander Br─Бhmaс╣Зas or the gods: Viс╣гс╣Зu, Brahm─Б, Rudra, ─Аditya, Agni, the protectors of the directions, or the planets. One should honour a Vaiс╣гс╣Зava and a previously initiated person.

In this verse and a half, the author explains the regulations. Previously initiated means someone who is older by oneself in order of initiation. One should honour and respect all these, the Br─Бhmaс╣Зas and so on, and never slander them. This is the meaning.

┬▓┬╣тБ╣After one has expounded the regulations, one should perform a fire sacrifice. One should place down the categories on the body of the disciple and purify it ^(220тАУ221)and then sacrifice into a blazing fire with the sixteen syllable mantra

Viс╣гс╣Зu.тАЩ He should then worship the Lord according to the path shown by the preceptor, release all the divinities, feed Br─Бhmaс╣Зas, present all the implements of the initiation to the preceptor and also honour his kinsmen.тАЭ

┬▓┬▓тБ╡O earth, even in a hundred years it is impossible to explain the greatness that comes from acting in this way.

The author explains the fruit of initiation in verses226тАУ234.

┬▓┬▓тБ╢If one becomes initiated by a preceptor and hears the Var─Бha, one has recited the Vedas, the Pur─Бс╣Зas, all the mantras and all the good compendia ┬▓┬▓тБ╖at the sacred Puс╣гkara T─лrtha, at Pray─Бga, Sindhus─Бgara, Devah┼лta,[^FNB000255] Kurukс╣гetra and especially V─Бr─Бс╣Зas─л. ┬▓┬▓тБ╕The fruit that the reciter attains from an eclipse or the equinox, that fruit is attained in the double by the initiate and by the listener. ┬▓┬▓тБ╣O bearer of all living beings! Even the gods engage in austerities, meditate and say: When will I be born in the land of Bh─Бrata? ┬▓┬│тБ░When will we become initiated? When will we hear the Var─Бha? Whenever Var─Бha, the self of the sixteen, is joined to the body, we will see the supreme destination, having once attained which one is not reborn.

Having studied the manual on initiation in the book Jayam─Бdhavam─Бnasoll─Бsa, I have written this commentary.

Var─Бha means the Var─Бha Pur─Бс╣Зa, the self or the shelter of the sixteen, the Pur─Бс╣Зas of Padma and so on, excepting the blessed Bh─Бgavata. Or else it means their originator, since it is celebrated as having appeared first from blessed Vy─Бsa. Joined to the body means connected to it through listening and so on. Or else it means making the Lord in the form of blessed Var─Бha, the self or the ruler of the sixteen categories, or having form of the sixteen sacrifices, burst forth through meditation and so on as if before oneтАЩs eyes, in the body consisting of the senses and so on beginning with the mind.

Instruction

In the Tattvas─Бra:[^FNB000259]

┬▓тБ┤тБ░If someone is unable to do even this, he should worship a lotus with unbroken rice and then anoint him with this water and the root mantra eight times. ┬▓тБ┤┬╣Placing his hand on the head [of the disciple], he should repeat it into his ear. This is the procedure for instructions. Simply relating the mantra at a solar or lunar eclipse, at a place of pilgrimage, in a place of the perfected ones or in a ┼Ъiva temple is called instruction.

[тАж]

For all of these instances, the N─Бrada Pa├▒car─Бtra gives some specifics (17.5тАУ10ab):

┬▓тБ┤┬▓A person of very small means but who is free from greed, who fears the terrors of repeated birth and death and who truly is a devotee of Viс╣гс╣ЗuтАФ┬▓тБ┤┬│the preceptor may grace such a one who lacks wealth with seeds offered together with ghee into the fire, just with water or with his words.

In verses242тАУ246 the author gives an exception to both the extended and shortened procedures given before. Seeds refer to barley and so on. [тАж]

рдпреЗрди рджрддреНрддреЗрди рдЪрд╛рдкреНрдиреЛрддрд┐ рд╢рд┐рд╡рдВ944 рдкрд░рдордХрд╛рд░рдгрдореН реереирелрежрее

Broo

the body [intact]; ┬▓тБ┤тБ╡who by his deeds, thoughts and words always gives fearlessness to the fearful; who has attained the stage of equal knowledge and who is also full of the Lord; ┬▓тБ┤тБ╢who is devoted to the five times;[^FNB000260] who knows the meaning of the Pa├▒car─Бtra; who has understood the truth of Viс╣гс╣Зu, one and divided into manyтАФhe can initiate the whole world, let alone the surrendered ones.

Now, how can the procedure for initiation be made complete? In order to reply to this doubt, the author writes verses244тАУ246. [тАж] The stage of equal knowledge means the stage of those of wisdom. Devoted to the five times means devoted to the duties of these times. Divided into many though one: this is with regard to the teaching of difference and nondifference.[^FNB000261] The surrendered ones are those who have taken shelter with devotion. This is the meaning.

The Greatness of Bestowing the Mantra

In a discussion between Brahm─Б and N─Бrada in the Sk─Бnda Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):

┬▓тБ┤тБ╖By giving this knowledge, a good person attains here fame, liberality, progeny, riches and happinessтАФthere is no doubt about it.

Knowledge here refers to the mantra, since it can bestow all the goals of man. The same word was used in the Kramad─лpik─Б (4.2), тАЬone truly desirous of knowledgeтАЭ. Fame means celebrity, liberality being generously disposed. Or else, both mean тАЬfamous for being liberalтАЭ, because of having given away this great gift. Good means guileless or faithful.

┬▓тБ┤тБ╕Just as Parame┼Ыvara is supreme among all the gods, so the gift of knowledge is known to be the greatest of all gifts. ┬▓тБ┤тБ╣Sin of even a hundred births is all destroyed when one bestows the gift of knowledge to men. ┬▓тБ╡тБ░There has never been and will never be a gift greater than the gift of knowledge. By this gift one attains ┼Ъiva, the supreme cause.

[тАж] ┼Ъiva means the auspicious one or the one who is supremely happy. The supreme cause means Brahman or blessed Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa.
